# Static-To-Proof Rebuild Transition Backlog

Status: active planning backlog
Last updated: 2026-06-16

This backlog records how the project moves from static closeout into scoped proof, tool, patch, mod, and rebuild work. It is not a runtime proof wave, visual QA wave, patch wave, Godot project, or rebuild parity claim.

## Static Closeout Anchor

| Track | Current |
| --- | --- |
| Static Ghidra function-quality closure | `6411/6411 = 100.00%` |
| Commentless / exact-undefined / `param_N` debt | `0 / 0 / 0` |
| Expanded post-100 static surface | `1560/1560 = 100.00%` |
| Active current-risk focused accounting | `1179/1179 = 100.00%` |
| Remaining active focused work | `0` |
| Wave911 focused | Historical-retired/non-reconstructable at `812/1408 = 57.67%` |
| Latest Ghidra review backup evidence ID | `BEA_20260607-230027_post_wave1219_final_score16_current_risk_review_verified` |

Static completion means the loaded Steam retail Ghidra database and active post-100 static lanes have closed under the current measurement contract. It does not mean runtime gameplay behavior, exact concrete layouts, BEA patching behavior, visual output, rebuild parity, or no-noticeable-difference parity have been proven.

## Claim Domains

| Domain | Current status | Authority |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Static Ghidra function quality | Closed | `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/static-reaudit-progress.json` |
| Active post-100 current-risk re-audit | Closed | `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/static-reaudit-current-risk-ledger.json` |
| System maps/contracts | Closed enough for transition planning | `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/mapped-systems.md` plus subsystem static contracts |
| Runtime behavior | Not started globally | Future copied-profile/app-owned proof slices only |
| Exact layouts / ABI | Open unless a contract proves a field role statically | Future layout proof packs |
| BEA patch behavior | Not started globally | Future byte-verified copied-profile patch bundles |
| Visual QA | Not started globally | Future screenshot/capture evidence sets |
| Rebuild parity | Not started | Future clean-room subsystem implementations and parity tests |
| No-noticeable-difference parity | Aspirational target, not proven | Requires later runtime, asset, visual, control, timing, save, patch, and rebuild proof |
| Godot sandbox | Parked | Installed outside repo; no active repo Godot project and not parity proof |

## Operating Rules

- Keep `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/static-reaudit-measurement-register.md` as the percentage front door.
- Keep `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/mapped-systems.md` as the implementation-facing static map front door.
- Treat historical wave paragraphs as at-wave evidence snapshots, not current progress.
- Start a runtime, visual, patch, Godot, or rebuild slice only after choosing one row from this backlog and writing its proof plan.
- Use copied profiles or app-owned artifact roots for generated outputs, caches, screenshots, frames, patches, or saves.
- Keep Codex root as final judgment. Each substantive objective or related release batch gets one review envelope: Codex `gpt-5.6-sol`/`ultra` normal/adversarial review plus bounded Cursor/Grok `grok-4.5-fast-xhigh` normal/adversarial consults when the required read-only sandbox and authentication are available. Routine follow-through does not recursively launch another envelope. Historical `no Cursor/Composer` wave notes remain evidence of how those earlier static/Ghidra waves were performed, not a forward prohibition on advisory consults.
